Inside the Guild, they keep their procedures close to their chests; and those who have been turned down by the Guild often have secrets of their own so don't want to talk to the press, not even to reputable prize-winning journalists like me.

Eventually, I found my way to a former under-secretary who used to work in the Guild's approvals department, until he was fired for using his work computer to view pictures of scantily-clad aliens. He was reluctant to talk to me and only agreed after I promised not to give his name, so we'll call him Brad.

Brad told me that potential applicants to the trading network have to submit detailed figures about the planet's economy, including their predicted imports and exports and the prices the exchange intends to set. This is all in the form of a multitude of complicated forms, of course - where would we be without all this red tape?

"Guild accountants look over all this huge mountain of paperwork," explained Brad, "which can take a great deal of time. Then they either approve the application or recommend further investigation. Either way, it's an incredibly slow process, although of course it can be sped up in the usual fashion." By which, of course, he meant the judicious application of some bribery, which will come as no surprise to readers of the Fed2 Star!

I pressed Brad on just what would cause an application to raise enough alarm bells to merit further investigation (other than a failure to bribe the right person, of course!) but he wouldn't give me any detail of what would make it deficient, no matter how much I probed. He did tell me what happens when investigation is merited.

"It's a rare occurrence, you understand - most applications are approved - but should that rare occurrence... erm... occur, then it was my department that despatched an accountant to the planet to investigate its economy and report back. Hir recommendations have the force of a final and binding decision so these accountants have a great deal of power. They are supposedly incorruptible, but who knows?"

I asked about the possibility of appeal, and Brad just laughed. "When I said final and binding, I meant it. Oh, there is an appeal process in place but no PO has ever managed to get a negative judgement overturned, not in all the time since the Guild started to have this kind of power."

I wanted Brad to introduce me to one of these special investigation accounts so I could get some more information about exactly how they go about things, but he seemed appalled at the very suggestion. Even as an ex-employee who left the Guild under a cloud, his loyalties remain with his former colleagues. He explained that the identity of the roving accountants was kept strictly confidential because their work was generally carried out undercover. I have to say I found the idea of undercover accountants very amusing - I can just picture spies with briefcases.

Having got all I could out of the helpful Brad, I resolved to continue to probe the way the Guild operates. Readers, next week I will bring you some background information about just how the Guild became so powerful.

============================================================
CHAPTER: COMMAND REFERENCE
============================================================

--- Overview ---
The following is a complete list of all Fed2 commands known at this time.


--- Accept ---
For low-ranking players, accepts a job offered by Armstrong Cuthbert or by a player.Usage: ACCEPT job#

Parameters: 'job#' is the number of the job on the workboard.Example: accept 5

Restrictions: Commanders and Captains only. You cannot accept a job if you don't have a ship.

To accept a pending job offered by a PO:

Usage: ACCEPT

To reject the job, use REJECT JOB.

For Plutocrats, accepts a membership bid to join your cartel.

Usage: ACCEPT systemname

Parameters: 'systemname' is the system you want to allow into your cartel.Example: accept rigel

Restrictions: Plutocrats only. The system must be in the pending queue for your cartel. You must be in the hub system for the cartel.

To reject a bid, use REJECT.

ACCEPT can be abbreviated to AC.


--- Act ---
Allows you to express any action or emotion.

Usage: ACT action

Parameters: 'action' is a word or phrase describing what you want other players to see.Example: act dances on the table

Players see: Newbod dances on the tableIf you are in your ship when you use the command, then your spaceship will carry out the act.

Example: act waggles its wings.

Players see: Newbod's spaceship waggles its wings.See also the ACTS command.


--- Acts ---
Allows you to express any action using a possessive.

Usage: ACTS action

Parameters: 'action' is a word or phrase describing what you want other players to see.Example: acts robot dances on the table

Players see: Newbod's robot dances on the tableSee also the ACT command.


--- Address ---
Give you the teleport address of the location you are in.

Usage: ADDRESS

Restrictions: You must be in possession of a teleporter.

You teleport using the TELEPORT command.


--- Akaturi ---
Asks for a job to carry valuable items for Armstrong Cuthbert.

Usage: AKATURI

Restrictions: Adventurers only. You must be in an Armstrong Cuthbert office.

AKATURI can be abbreviated to AK.


--- Allocate ---
Docks a Blish City with a planet.

Usage: ALLOCATE cityname TO planetname

Parameters: 'cityname' is the name of the city you want to dock.'Planetname' is the destination planet.Example: allocate nutbush city to church house

Restrictions: Plutocrats only. The planet must be in the same star system as the Blish city.


--- Ansi ---
The game normally strips out any ANSI color codes that it received, but you can use this command to turn on the receipt of color codes.

Usage: ANSI on|off

Parameters: 'on' turns on the receipt of ANSI color codes, in other words it stops the game stripping them out. 'off' turns it off again.The setting only lasts for your game session.


--- Approve ---
Approves a bid from a Financier to buy shares in your business.

Usage: APPROVE BID bid#

Parameters: 'bid#' is the number of the bid.Example: approve bid 2

Restrictions: Industrialists only.

To reject a bid, use REJECT.


--- Assign ---
Moves workthings from one planet in your star system to another.

Usage: ASSIGN xx WORKERS FROM planetname TO planetname

Parameters: 'xx' is the number of workers you want to move.'planetname' is the planet you want to move the workers from and to.Example: ASSIGN 100 WORKERS FROM RIGEL 4 TO RIGEL 5

Restrictions: Magnates only. You must have built ten airports on your planet and then upgraded them - see UPGRADE AIRPORT. You can only move workthings that are not already employed.


--- Attack ---
Initiates an attack on another player.

Conditions: You must have set another player as your target, the target must be in the same location as you. You can only attack in space, but not in orbit or at a link.


--- Bid ---
Puts in a bid to buy shares in a business.

Usage: BID amount SHARES AT shareprice IN businessname

Parameters: 'amount' is the number of shares you want to buy.'shareprice' is the price you want to pay for them.'businessname' is the name of the business you want to invest in.Example: bid 150 shares at 10000 in Newbod Enterprises

Restrictions: you must be a Financier. You have to buy at least 150 shares each purchase. Your shareholding in the business cannot exceed 1,000. Your total portfolio cannot exceed 35,000.


--- Block ---
Blocks communications from annoying players, so you do not see any messages originating from them.

Usage: BLOCK playername

Parameters: 'playername' is the annoying player you want to block.Example: block dork

You can only block players who are in the game. The block lasts for your game session. To receive the player's messages again, use UNBLOCK.

BLOCK on its own lists the players you are currently ignoring.


--- Board shuttle ---
Allows you to take a shuttle from your ship to a planet, and back again.

Usage: BOARD SHUTTLE

Restrictions: you must have a ship. You must either be on a landing pad, or in orbit around a planet.

BOARD SHUTTLE can be abbreviated to BOARD.


--- Bribe ---
Offers a bribe to a Galactic Administration official or a person in a position to provide a service - which is often the only way to get what you want.

Usage: BRIBE name

Parameters: 'name' is the person you want to bribe.


--- Brief ---
Turns on brief descriptions. When you move into a location you will only see the name of the room, plusany objects, mobiles, or players in the location.

Usage: BRIEF

The FULL command turns full descriptions back on.


--- Build ---
Builds infrastructure on your planet or in your cartel to enhance the economy.

Usage: BUILD infrastructure [commodity]

Parameters: 'infrastructure' is the type of infrastructure you want to build'commodity' is a parameter needed for some builds, specifying which commodity should be enhanced by the buildExample: build heliograph woods

Cost for planet builds: 10 meg.

Cartel build costs vary.Restrictions: Planet-owners and plutocrats only. POs must be on the planet.

Some builds can only be built at certain levels; some can only be built after other builds.


--- Build city ---
Builds a Blish City in your cartel.

Usage: BUILD CITY cityname

Parameters: 'cityname' is what you want to call the city.Example: build city Nutbush City

Once the basic city has been built, you can increase the size by doing a further build.

Usage: BUILD CITY

When the city has reached your required size you fit it out.

Usage: BUILD CITY level

Parameters: 'level' is the economic level you want the city to operate at, either agri, resource, ind, tech or leisure.Restrictions: Plutocrats only. Your cartel must have a graving dock.


--- Buy commodity ---
Buys a 75-ton container of goods from a trading exchange.

Usage: BUY commodity

Parameters: 'commodity' is the item you wish to buy.Restrictions: You must be in a trading exchange, and you must be a Merchant.


--- Buy depot ---
Buys a depot on the planet you are on.

Usage: BUY DEPOT

Restrictions: Industrialists and Manufacturers only. You must be in an exchange. Industrialists are limited to 16 depots.


--- Buy factory ---
Buys a factory on the planet you are on, to produce the specified commodity.

Usage: BUY FACTORY commodity

Parameters: 'commodity' is the output you want the factory to produce.Example: buy factory crystals

Restrictions: Industrialists and Manufacturers only. Industrialists can own up to 8 factories, Manufacturers up to 15. You must be in an exchange.


--- Buy food ---
Replenishes your stamina.

Usage: BUY FOOD

Restrictions: you must be in a bar.

Costs 10 IG. Increases current stamina by 5 points.


--- Buy fuel ---
Fills up your ship's fuel tank.

Usage: BUY FUEL

Restrictions: only works if you have a ship.

Costs 10 IG per ton when you are on the ground, 50 IG per ton in space.You can also specify the amount of fuel you want to buy.

Usage: BUY tons FUEL

Parameters: 'tons' is the number of tons you want to buy.


--- Buy futures ---
Buys a futures contract from a trading exchange.

Usage: BUY FUTURES commodity

Parameters: 'commodity' is the item in which you wish to buy a futures contract.Restrictions: You must be in a trading exchange, and you must be a Trader.


--- Buy missiles ---
Purchases missiles to be used during a battle.

Usage: BUY MISSILES

This fills up your missile magazineUsage: BUY number MISSILES

Parameter: 'number' is the number of missiles you want to buyCosts 5,000 IG each

You must have a missile rack installed in your ship, and have room for missiles in your magazine. Can only be bought in a weapons shop.


--- Buy pizza ---
Allows you to feed everyone in the bar.

Usage: BUY PIZZA flavor

Parameters: 'flavor' is a word or phrase describing what you want to buy people. If you don't specify a flavor of pizza, you purchase the standard house pizza.Example: buy pizza a large plate of jellied eels

Players see: Newbod has bought you a large plate of jellied eelsRestrictions: you must be in a bar.

Costs 10 IG per pizza. Increases current stamina by 5 points.


--- Buy registry ---
Purchases a ship registration facility so that any ships bought on your planet become part of your merchant fleet.

Usage: BUY REGISTRY

Costs 5 slithy toves.


--- Buy round ---
Allows you to buy a drink for everyone in the bar.

Usage: BUY ROUND drink

Parameters: 'drink' is a word or phrase describing what you want to buy people. If you don't specify a drink, you purchase a round of the house beverage.Example: buy round a large glass of Jack Daniels

Players see: Newbod has bought you a large glass of Jack DanielsRestrictions: you must be in a bar.

Costs 5 IG per drink. Increases current stamina by 2 points.


--- Buy sensors/jammers ---
Adds sensors or jammers to your ship.

Usage: BUY number sensors|jammers

Parameters: 'number' is the number of sensors you want to buy.'sensors|jammers' is where you specify which of the two things you want to buyexample: buy 3 sensors

Restrictions: only works if you have a ship.

You must be in a repair shop.Costs 10,000 IG each, and each sensor or jammer takes up 2 tons of cargo space.


--- Buy shares ---
Increases your personal shareholding in your business.

Usage: BUY SHARES amount AT shareprice

Parameters: 'amount' is the number of shares you want to buy.'shareprice' is the price you want to pay for them.Example: buy shares 150 at 8000

Restrictions: you must be an Industrialist. You have to buy at least 150 shares each purchase. Your shareholding cannot exceed 1,000.

Manufacturers can also buy more shares to increase your personal shareholding in your company.

Usage: BUY amount SHARES

Parameters: 'amount' is the number of shares you want to buy.Example: buy 10 shares

Restrictions: Manufacturers only. You can only buy 100 shares at a time, up to a limit of 2,000.

Financiers can buy shares in other companies.

Usage: BUY amount SHARES name

Parameters: 'name' is the name of the CEO or the name of the companyExample: buy 100 shares Newbod Industries

Restrictions: You can only buy 100 shares at a time. The broker will always keep 1,000 shares.


--- Buy ship ---
Purchases a spaceship.

Usage: BUY SHIP

Restrictions: only works in a shipyard.

GroundHogs will be offered the starter special. Captains and above can custom order a ship to their specifications, trading in the old ship as part of the deal.Click here to read the Jarrow pricelist.


--- Buy stat ---
Boosts one of your stats by one point.

Usage: BUY statname

Parameters: 'statname' is the stat you want to improve: stamina, strength, dexterity or intelligence.Cost: 1 slithy tove.

Restrictions: You must be in the right location for each stat boost. There is a limit of 150 on all stats. You can only purchase one stat boost per day.


--- Buy treasury ---
Increases your company's treasury stock.

Usage: BUY amount TREASURY

Parameters: 'amount' is the number of shares you want the company to buy.Example: buy 10 TREASURY

Restrictions: Manufacturers only. You can only buy 100 shares at a time, up to a limit of 2,000.


--- Buy warehouse ---
Purchases a warehouse on the planet you are on.

Usage: BUY WAREHOUSE

Cost: 650,000 IG.

Restrictions: You must be in an exchange. You must have a building permit.

WAREHOUSE can be abbreviated to WARE.


--- Calendar ---
Tells you which event runs on which day.

Usage: CALENDAR


--- Call staff ---
Alerts any staff members in the game that you need help.

Usage: CALL STAFF


--- Cancel events ---
Switches off the notification of things which happen in the Solar System affecting exchange prices.

Usage: CANCEL EVENTS


--- Carry ---
Displays an object in your inventory so that other players see it when they look at you.

Usage: CARRY objectname

Parameters: 'objectname' is the name of the object you want to display when other players examine you.Take it off again with POCKET. See also WEAR and DOFF, CLIP and UNCLIP.


--- Change clothes ---
Personalizes your character's description.

Usage: CHANGE CLOTHES description

Parameters: 'description' is what people see when they examine you.Example: change clothes You see a space cadet wearing a brand new spacesuit

Players examining you see: You see a space cadet wearing a brand new spacesuitRestrictions: Limit of 220 characters.

Costs 10 IG.


--- Change desc ---
Changes the description of the location you are standing in.

Usage: CHANGE DESC new_desc

Parameters: 'new_desc' is what you want the description of the location to change to.Example: change desc The room is decorated with memorabilia from Big Bertha's childhood. There's a picture of her being crowned Junior Miss Cargon, together with the sash she wore for the competition, and another picture which shows her shaking hands with the Emperor Ming! Bertha herself stands behind the bar ready to serve you drinks or to reminisce about her past glories.

Restrictions: You must be the owner of the planet. The change only lasts until the next reset unless you SAVE MAP. The changed description can only have one paragraph, and is limited to the command input size.


--- Change fighting ---
Toggles the fighting property on and off a space location, to allow ship fighting (or not).

Usage: CHANGE FIGHTING

Restrictions: Space locations only. Cannot be used in orbit or link locations. You must be the owner of the system. The change only lasts until the next reset unless you SAVE MAP.


--- Change name ---
Changes the name of the location you are standing in.

Usage: CHANGE NAME new_name

Parameters: 'new_name' is what you want the name of the location to change to.Example: change name Big Bertha's Bar

Restrictions: You must be the owner of the planet. The change only lasts until the next reset unless you SAVE MAP.


--- Cheat ---
What it says!

Usage: CHEAT


--- Check price ---
Check the price of a commodity in an exchange.

Usage: CHECK PRICE commodity

Parameters: 'commodity' is the item on which you want to check the price.Restrictions: You must be in a trading exchange.

CHECK can be abbreviated to C.

Traders can use the command to check the price remotely for items in which they hold a futures contract.

Usage: CHECK PRICE commodity planetname

Parameters: 'commodity' is the item on which you want to check the price.'planetname' is the exchange from which the contract was bought.Merchants and above can pay a slithy tove at the brokers office on Earth, and use this command to get remote prices on all commodities for 31 days. The command is BUY REMOTE SERVICE.

It can also be used to get prices from all the planets in the cartel you are in:

Usage: CHECK PRICE commodity CARTELBut it won't work in Sol.There is an upgrade to this service for a one-off cost of two slithies, which allows you to get the price for a commodity on all the Sol planets, and a whole commodity group on a planet. The command is UPGRADE REMOTE SERVICE.

Usage: CHECK PRICE commodity

Parameters: 'commodity' is the item on which you want to check the price.Restrictions: This only works outside an exchange.

Usage: CHECK PRICE commoditygroup planetname

Parameters: 'commoditygroup' is agri, resource, ind, tech, biological or leisure.'planetname' is the planet you want to check the prices on.The premium ticker service which costs five slithy toves gives the price of a commodity on all planets with the command C PREMIUM commodity.


--- Check premium ---
Check the price of a commodity on all planets in the Galaxy.

Usage: CHECK PREMIUM commodity buy|sell|all

Parameters: 'commodity' is the item on which you want to check the price.'buy|sell|all' determines whether you see the buying prices, the selling prices or all the prices (which is a very long list!). Leaving this off defaults to showing all the prices.Example: c PREMIUM droids buy

Restrictions: You must have a premium ticker, which costs five slithy toves and can be bought from anywhere with the command BUY PREMIUM TICKER. The premium ticker will only work if you have the remote price subscription available from TC&B on Earth.

CHECK can be abbreviated to C.


--- Clear ---
Removes your mood, or stops targetting a player.

Usage: CLEAR MOOD

Usage: CLEAR TARGET


--- Claim ---
Automatically links a stock planet into the game, to promote to Founder at the next reset.

Usage: CLAIM SYSTEM systemname PLANET planetname TYPE stocksystemname

Parameters: 'systemname' is the name you want to give your system.

'planetname'is the name you want to give your planet.'stocksystemname' is the type of stock planet you want to use. The options are: beach, furnace, iceberg, rescue, stone, sweet.Example: claim system big star planet new world type sweet

Restrictions: Financiers only. You can only use the command once.

System and planet names can be up to 32 characters, and can contain spaces. You can use letters and numbers, but no punctuation or symbols, and they must start with a letter. They must not already exist in the game. Do not use the words system, planet or type as part of the names.

The new planet will be linked into the game at the next reset which will promote you to Founder.

Warning: make sure you have spelled the system and planet names correctly before you press return, because you can't change them once you have issued the command!


--- Clip ---
Selects which of your charms you want to attach to your keyring (although it can be used with any object).

Usage: CLIP objectname

Parameters: 'objectname' is the name of the charm you want to display.Remove it with UNCLIP. See also WEAR and DOFF, CARRY and POCKET.

Restrictions: you can only clip charms to your keyring.


--- Close link ---
Closes a system so that nobody can jump to it.

Usage: CLOSE LINK

Restrictions: You must be the owner of the system. The command must be used when you are in space.


--- Close range ---
Moves your ship closer to your opponent during a fight, allowing you to use lasers.

Usage: CLOSE RANGE

Restrictions: you must have attacked, or been attacked by, another player, and be in open or intermediate range.


--- Collect ---
Arranges for cargo to be loaded into your ship.

Usage: COLLECT

Restrictions: you must be in the Armstrong Cuthbert office on the right planet to collect the cargo.


--- Colonize ---
Automatically links a new stock planet into an existing star system, which will appear at the next reset.

Usage: COLONIZE PLANET planetname TYPE stockplanetname

Parameters: 'planetname'is the name you want to give your planet.

'stockplanetname' is the type of stock planet you want to use. The options are: water, fire, ice, habitat, rock or my favourite, candy.Example: colonize planet new world 2 type fire

The command can be spelled with an S or a Z.

Restrictions: This only works to add a second or third planet. Subsequent planets will be allowed later. You must be a Mogul or above to link a second planet, and Gengineer or above for a third planet.

Your space map must have the link in location 460, and the location for the new planet must be empty - 461 for the second planet and 397 for the third.

Planet names can be up to 32 characters, and can contain spaces. You can use letters and numbers, but no punctuation or symbols, and they must start with a letter. They must not already exist in the game. Do not use the words system, planet or type as part of the names.

The new planet will be linked into the game at the next reset.

Warning: make sure you have spelled the planet name correctly before you press return, because you can't change it once you have issued the command!


--- Comms ---
Controls your communications unit.

Usage: COMMS on|off

Parameters: 'on' turns your comms unit on; 'off' turns it off. COMMS on its own tells you if it's on or off.


--- Communicate ---
Sends a message to all players in the game.

Usage: COMMUNICATE message

Parameters: 'message' is the message you want to send.Example: communicate Hello, where's the party?

Players see: Your comm unit crackles with a message from Newbod, "Hello, where's the party"COMMUNICATE can be abbreviated to COMM or COM.


--- Cuddle ---
Cuddles another player.

Usage: CUDDLE playername

Parameters: 'playername' is the name of the person you want to cuddle.Note: the game adds a random qualifier.

See also GROPE, HUG, KISS, SMILE, SNOG, and TICKLE.


--- Declare bankruptcy ---
Demotes Merchants back to Adventurer, Industrialists to Trader, Manufacturers to Industrialist and Financiers to Manufacturer.

Usage: DECLARE BANKRUPTCY

Restrictions: Merchants, Industrialists, Manufacturers and Financiers only.


--- Deliver ---
Arranges delivery of the goods you are hauling as a job.

Usage: DELIVER

Restrictions: you must be in the Armstrong Cuthbert office on the destination planet to deliver the cargo.


--- Demolish ---
Demolishes infrastructure on your planet, to clear the way for new builds.

Usage: DEMOLISH infrastructure

Parameters: 'infrastructure' is the infrastructure build you want to demolish.Example: demolish weather

You will get back between 3 and 7 meg for the demolished build.

Restrictions: Planet-owners only. You must be on the planet.

Some infrastructure cannot be demolished until after you can no longer build replacements: heliograph, telegraph, base, satellite, defence and oil.


--- Deposit a bond ---
Promotes you to Trader.

Usage: DEPOSIT A BOND

Restrictions: Merchants only. You must be in the TC&B offices on Earth, and have the promotion requirements.


--- Display accounts ---
Shows you your company's accounts.

Usage: DISPLAY ACCOUNTS

Restrictions: Manufacturers and Financiers only.

Financiers can also look at the accounts for other companies:

Usage: DISPLAY ACCOUNTS name

Parameters: 'name' is the name of the CEO or the name of the company.Example: display accounts newbod

Restrictions: Financiers only.

DISPLAY can be abbreviated to DI.


--- Display akaturi ---
Displays the details of your Akaturi job.

Usage: DISPLAY AKATURI

DISPLAY can be abbreviated to DI and AKATURI to AK.


--- Display business ---
Displays the details of your business.

Usage: DISPLAY BUSINESS

Restrictions: Industrialists only.

Other players can get limited information about your business:

Usage: DISPLAY BUSINESS businessname

Example: display business Newbod Enterprises

Restrictions: Traders and above only.

DISPLAY can be abbreviated to DI.


--- Display businesses ---
Lists all the businesses in the game.

Usage: DISPLAY BUSINESSES

DISPLAY can be abbreviated to DI.


--- Display cartel ---
Gives information about a cartel, including the names of the systems it contains. If you do not specify a cartel, the game will give you information about the cartel you are currently in.

Usage: DISPLAY CARTEL

Usage: DISPLAY CARTEL cartelname

Parameters: 'cartelname' is the name of the star system on which you want info.Example: display cartel scratchwood

DISPLAY can be abbreviated to DI.


--- Display cartels ---
Lists all of the cartels in the game.

Usage: DISPLAY CARTELS

DISPLAY can be abbreviated to DI.


--- Display CEO ---
Tells you who owns a business or company.

Usage: DISPLAY CEO name

Parameters: 'name' is the business or company whose owner you want to know about.Example: display ceo universal exports

DISPLAY can be abbreviated to DI.


--- Display channel ---
Lists the communications channels in the game.

Usage: DISPLAY CHANNEL

You can also see the details for one channel by including the name of the channel.

Usage: DISPLAY CHANNEL channelname

Parameters: 'channelname' is the name of the channel you want details on.Example: display channel trader talk

DISPLAY can be abbreviated to DI and CHANNEL to CH.


--- Display companies ---
Lists all the companies in the game.

Usage: DISPLAY COMPANIES

DISPLAY can be abbreviated to DI.


--- Display company ---
Displays the details of your company.

Usage: DISPLAY COMPANY

Restrictions: Manufacturers and Financiers only.

DISPLAY can be abbreviated to DI.


--- Display disaffection ---
Displays the way your disaffection or approval rating was calculated at the last reset.

Usage: DISPLAY DISAFFECTION

Restrictions: you must be a planet-owner, and you must be somewhere on your planet.

DISPLAY can be abbreviated to DI.


--- Display depot ---
Displays your depot on the specified planet, listing the contents.

Usage: DISPLAY DEPOT planetname

Parameters: 'planetname' is the planet on which the depot is sited.Example: display depot titan

Restrictions: Industrialists and Manufacturers only.

DISPLAY can be abbreviated to DI.


--- Display email ---
Displays the registered email address for your account.

Usage: DISPLAY EMAIL

DISPLAY can be abbreviated to DI.


--- Display events ---
Lists the last 30 things that have happened in the Solar System (since the start of the game session) affecting exchange prices.

Usage: DISPLAY EVENTS

You can limit the list to just one planet.

Usage: DISPLAY EVENTS planetname

Parameters: 'planetname' is the planet you want to see the events for.Example: display events Mars

DISPLAY can be abbreviated to DI.


--- Display exchange ---
Displays the exchange information for your planet.

Usage: DISPLAY EXCHANGE

The display can be restricted to one commodity group:

Usage: DISPLAY EXCHANGE commoditygroup

Parameters: 'commoditygroup' is agri, resource, ind, tech, biological, leisure, bulk, consumer, defence, energy or sea.Example: display exchange agri

Restrictions: you must be a planet-owner, and you must be somewhere on your planet.

The command can also be used remotely:

Usage: DISPLAY EXCHANGE planetname

DISPLAY EXCHANGE commoditygroup planetnameParameters: 'planetname' is the name of your planet.DISPLAY can be abbreviated to DI.


--- Display factory ---
Displays the specified factory.

Usage: DISPLAY FACTORY factory#

Parameters: 'factory#' is the number of the factory that you want to display.Example: display factory 3

Restrictions: Industrialists and Manufacturers only.

DISPLAY can be abbreviated to DI.


--- Display factories ---
Shows you the status of all the factories on your planet - whether they are running, where the output is directed, and the efficiency.

Usage: DISPLAY FACTORIES

Restrictions: Planet-owners only. You must be on your planet.

The command can also be used remotely:

Usage: DISPLAY FACTORIES planetname

Parameters: 'planetname' is the name of your planet.DISPLAY can be abbreviated to DI.


--- Display fleet ---
Shows you the owners of the ships registered on your planet.

Usage: DISPLAY FLEET

Restrictions: Planet-owners only. You must be on your planet.

DISPLAY can be abbreviated to DI.


--- Display futures ---
In an exchange, the command lists all the futures contracts available from that exchange. Outside an exchange, the command lists all the futures contracts you hold.

Usage: DISPLAY FUTURES

You can modify the display of your contracts to show just those for a particular commodity, or a particular planet:

Usage: DISPLAY FUTURES commodity

Parameters: 'commodity' is the item for which you wish to see all your contracts.Usage: DISPLAY FUTURES planetname

Parameters: 'planetname' is the planet for which you wish to see all your contracts.Restrictions: You must be in a trading exchange, and you must be a Trader.

DISPLAY can be abbreviated to DI.


--- Display graving ---
Shows the progress of a graving dock build.

Usage: DISPLAY GRAVING

Restrictions: Plutocrats only. You must have issued the command to build a graving dock.

DISPLAY can be abbreviated to DI.


--- Display infra ---
Displays the infrastructure details for the named planet. If you do not specify a planet, the game will give you information about the planet you are currently on.

Usage: DISPLAY INFRA

Usage: DISPLAY INFRA planetname

Parameters: 'planetname' is the name of the planet for which you want to display the builds.Example: display infra bodville

DISPLAY can be abbreviated to DI.


--- Display locker ---
Displays the contents of your ship storage locker.

Usage: DISPLAY LOCKER

DISPLAY can be abbreviated to DI.

Restrictions: you must be in your ship.

Use STASH to put objects into your locker and RETRIEVE to get them back again.


--- Display louie ---
Gives a report on the game of Lucky Louie you are currently playing.

Usage: DISPLAY LOUIE

DISPLAY can be abbreviated to DI.


--- Display planet ---
Displays the details for the named planet. If you own the planet, it also gives information about the economy. If you do not specify a planet, the game will give you information about the planet you are currently on.

Usage: DISPLAY PLANET

Usage: DISPLAY PLANET planetname

Parameters: 'planetname' is the name of the planet you want to display.Example: display planet titan

DISPLAY can be abbreviated to DI.

Displays the way your workforce was calculated at the last reset.

Usage: DISPLAY POPULATION

Restrictions: you must be a planet-owner, and you must be somewhere on your planet.

DISPLAY can be abbreviated to DI.

Displays the production and consumption figures for your planet.

Usage: DISPLAY PRODUCTION commoditygroup

Parameters: 'commoditygroup' is agri, resource, ind, tech, biological or leisure, bulk, consumer, defence, energy or sea.Example: display production agri

Restrictions: you must be a planet-owner, and you must be somewhere on your planet.

The command can also be used remotely:

Usage: DISPLAY PRODUCTION commoditygroup planetname

Parameters: 'planetname' is the name of your planet.DISPLAY can be abbreviated to DI.

Gives information about a star system, including the names of the planets it contains. If you do not specify a system, the game will give you information about the system you are currently in.

Lists all of the open systems in the game.

You can also see all of the systems, including the closed ones.
