--- Display warehouse ---
Lists all of your warehouses.

Usage: DISPLAY WAREHOUSE

The command will also list the contents of a specific warehouse.

Usage: DISPLAY WAREHOUSE planetname

Parameters: 'planetname' is the planet on which the warehouse you are interested in resides.Example: display warehouse mars

DISPLAY can be abbreviated to DI and WAREHOUSE to WARE.


--- Divert ---
Diverts commodites that are sold or delivered to the exchange, so if they are needed for the build, they go into the graving dock warehouse instead of into the stocks.

Usage: DIVERT

Restrictions: Plutocrats only. You must have a graving dock.

Turn the diversion off with UNDIVERT.


--- Divorce ---
Dissolves your marriage to another player.

Usage: DIVORCE

Restrictions: You must be in the registry office on Earth - your spouse does not need to be present.

Cost: 2 slithy tove.


--- Doff ---
Removes an object that you are wearing.

Usage: DOFF objectname

Parameters: 'objectname' is the name of the object you want to remove.See also WEAR, CARRY and POCKET, CLIP and UNCLIP.


--- Drop ---
Drops an object you are holding.

Usage: DROP object

Parameters: 'object' is an object you are holding.Restrictions: you must be holding the specified object.

Usage: DROP objectname


--- Dropoff ---
Delivers an akatari package.

Usage: DROPOFF

You must be in the location which is the destination for the package.


--- Examine ---
Shows you the description of a player or an object, or shows you a display cabinet.

Usage: EXAMINE playername

Parameters: 'playername' is the name of a player.Usage: EXAMINE objectname

Parameters: 'objectname' is the name of an object.Restrictions: the player must be in the same location as you; the object must in the same location or in your inventory.

The command alsohows you the display cabinet belonging to the star system you are in.

Usage: EXAMINE CABINET

Restrictions: you must be on a landing pad.

EXAMINE can be abbreviated to EX.

Use EXAMINE ME to look at yourself - this will also list all of your keyring charms.


--- Exile ---
Gives a list of all the planets and who has been exiled from them. POs can use the command to banish a player from your star system, so he cannot jump through the link. If he is in your system, it moves him to Earth.

Usage: EXILE

Usage: EXILE playername

Parameters: 'playername' is the name of the player you want to exile.Restrictions: Planet-owners only. You must be somewhere in your star system.

Note: Use PARDON to rescind the banishment.


--- Expel ---
Kicks a star system out of your cartel and puts it into the Sol cartel.

Usage: EXPEL systemname

Parameters: 'systemname' is the name of the star system you want to get rid of.Restrictions: Plutocrats only. You must be somewhere in your star system. The star system must be a member of your cartel.


--- Expropriate depot ---
Gets rid of an unwanted depot on your planet.

Usage: EXPROPRIATE DEPOT companyname

Parameters: 'companyname' is the name of the company that owns the depot.Example: expropriate depot universal exports

Restrictions: Planet-owners only. You must be on the planet.


--- Expropriate factory ---
Gets rid of an unwanted factory on your planet.

Usage: EXPROPRIATE FACTORY factory# companyname

Parameters: 'factory#' is the number of the factory'companyname' is the name of the company that owns the factory.Example: expropriate factory 2 universal exports

Restrictions: Planet-owners only. You must be on the planet.


--- Extend cabinet ---
Expandes your display cabinet by adding 13 extra slots.

Usage: EXTEND CABINET

Cost: 1 slithy tove.

Restrictions: planet-owners only. You must be in your system.


--- Fed2 ---
Gives a bit of information about the game.

Usage: FED2


--- Fetch ---
Moves a container of goods from the warehouse on the planet you are on, into your ship's cargo hold.

Usage: FETCH #

Parameters: '#' is the bay number that contains the goods, as shown on the warehouse display.


--- Fire ---
Fires a laser at your opponent during a ship fight.

Usage: FIRE weapon

Parameters: 'weapon' is the type of laser you want to fire: laser, tl or ql

Restrictions: You must be in space, in a fighting location. You must have set a target, and the player you are targetting must in the same location. You must be in close range.

FIRE MISSILE can also be used as an alternative to LAUNCH MISSILE.


--- Flee ---
Moves you directly to the interstellar link, but damages it on the way. For use if you want to make a quick escape when your ship is attacked.

Usage: FLEE

Restrictions: only works at open range or intermediate range. Your ship will take damage.


--- Flush factory ---
Clears the specified factory's storeroom, sending the accumulated goods on to their destination.

Usage: FLUSH FACTORY factory#

Parameters: 'factory#' is the number of the factory that you want to flush.Example: flush factory 3

Restrictions: Industrialists and Manufacturers only.


--- Freeze ---
Puts your company into stasis until the next time you log on.

Usage: FREEZE COMPANY

Cost: 500,000ig (from your personal balance).

Restrictions: company owners only.


--- Full ---
Turns on full descriptions. This means that when you move into a location you will see the complete description, along with any objects, mobiles, or players in the location.

Usage: FULL

The BRIEF command turns brief descriptions on.


--- Get ---
Picks up an object.

Usage: GET objectname

Parameters: 'objectname' is the name of the object you want to pick up.Restrictions: you must be in the same location as the object.


--- Give ---
Gives groats, a slithy or an object to another player.

Usage: GIVE playername amount

Parameters: 'playername' is the name of the person you want to give the groats to.'amount' is the number of groats you want to give.Restrictions: A player cannot receive more than 1,000IG in a day.

Usage: GIVE playername SLITHY

Parameters: 'playername' is the name of the person you want to give the slithy to.Usage: GIVE playername objectname

Parameters: 'playername' is the name of the person you want to give the object to.'objectname' is the name of the object you want to give.Example: give newbod top hat


--- Glance ---
Shows you the short description of the location you are in, and lists the players present. Can also be used to check other players' moods.

Usage: GLANCE

The command can also be used to show you somebody's mood.

Usage: GLANCE playername

Parameters: 'playername' is the name of the person whose mood you want to see.To see the moods of all players in your location, use 'GLANCE ALL'.


--- Goto ---
Moves you automatically between planets.

Usage: GOTO planetname

Parameters: 'planetname' is the planet you want to go to.Restrictions: The command only works from planetary orbit, and only in the Solar System.

You must upgrade your navigation computer to get access to this command.


--- Grope ---
Gropes another player.

Usage: GROPE playername

Parameters: 'playername' is the name of the person you want to grope.Note: the game adds a random qualifier.

See also CUDDLE, HUG, KISS, SMILE, SNOG, and TICKLE.


--- Hide ---
Conceals an object in your display cabinet.

Usage: HIDE objectname

Parameters: 'objectname' is an object in your inventory.Restrictions: you must be the PO of the star system you are in.

Use RETRIEVE to get objects back out and DISPLAY LOCKER or EXAMINE CABINET to see what is in the locker or cabinet.


--- Hug ---
Hugs another player.

Usage: HUG playername

Parameters: 'playername' is the name of the person you want to hug.Note: the game adds a random qualifier.

You can hug people who are not in the same room as you.

See also CUDDLE, GROPE, KISS, SMILE, SNOG, and TICKLE.


--- Insure ---
Insures your life against one death. If you die while insured you will wake up in a hospital. Your score tells you whether you are insured or not, and if not, how much it will cost you to remedy that situation.

Usage: INSURE

Cost goes up each insurance


--- IPO ---
Checks the effect floating your company would have on the stock market.

Usage: IPO markup

Parameters: 'markup' is the markup on the book value of the company that you want to apply.Example: ipo 10

Restrictions: You must be an Industrialist. The markup must be between -20 and 20.

To actually go ahead with the IPO, use LAUNCH IPO.


--- Inventory ---
Lists the items in your possession: first the things in your permanent kit, which stay with you throughout the game, and then any objects you have found.

Usage: INVENTORY

Inventory can be abbreviated to I or INV.


--- Issue dividend ---
Pays a dividend to all the company's shareholders.

Usage: ISSUE DIVIDEND amount

Parameters: 'amount' is the number of groats you want to pay out per share.Example: issue dividend 5

Restrictions: Manufacturers and Financiers only. There is an upper limit on 2,000 groats per share, and the command can only be used twice a day.


--- Jobs ---
Toggles on and off the notification of new work from Armstrong Cuthbert.

Usage: JOBS on|off

Parameters: 'on' turns the job notifications on; 'off' turns them off.Having jobs turned on registers you for work with Armstrong Cuthbert, so jobs will be generated for your particular cargo size.


--- Join cartel ---
Puts in an application for your star system to join a cartel.

Usage: JOIN CARTEL cartelname

Parameters: 'cartelname' is the name of the cartel you want to join.Restrictions: you must be a planet-owner. You must be in your star system.


--- Join channel ---
Joins an existing communications channel or starts a new one.

Usage: JOIN CHANNEL channelname

Parameters: 'channelname' is the name of the channel you want to tune to.CHANNEL can be abbreviated to CH.


--- Join louie ---
Joins a game of game of Lucky Louie.

Usage: START LOUIE playername

Parameters: 'playername' is the name of the player whose game you want to join.Example: join louie hazed

Restrictions: A game of Lucky Louie can only have three people in it.


--- Jump ---
Tells you which other star systems you can visit from your current system, and lets you travel through hyperspace to reach them.

Usage: JUMP

Usage: JUMP systemname

Parameters: 'systemname' is the name of the star system which you want to go to.Example: jump rigel

JUMP can be abbreviated to J.

Restrictions: you must be at an Interstellar Link, and have at least 50 hauling credits. You can only jump to another cartel via the hub systems of the cartels.


--- Kiss ---
Kisses another player.

Usage: KISS playername

Parameters: 'playername' is the name of the person you want to kiss.Note: the game adds a random qualifier.

You can kiss people who are not in the same room as you.

See also CUDDLE, GROPE, HUG, SMILE, SNOG, and TICKLE.


--- Launch IPO ---
Floats your company on the stock market.

Usage: LAUNCH IPO markup

Parameters: 'markup' is the markup on the book value of the company that you want to apply.Example: launch ipo 10

Restrictions: You must be an Industrialist. The markup must be between -20 and 20.


--- Launch missile ---
Fires a missile at another ship.

Usage: LAUNCH MISSILE

Restrictions: You must be in space, in a fighting location. You must have set a target, and the player you are targetting must in the same location. You must have a missile to launch.


--- Leave channel ---
Leaves the communications channel you are tuned to.

Usage: LEAVE CHANNEL

Parameters: 'channelname' is the name of the channel you want to tune to.CHANNEL can be abbreviated to CH.


--- Leave louie ---
Leaves a game of game of Lucky Louie.

Usage: LEAVE LOUIE


--- Liquidate commodity ---
Closes out a futures contract in the specified commodity.

Usage: LIQUIDATE commodity

Parameters: 'commodity' is the contract you wish to liquidate.Restrictions: You must be in a trading exchange, and you must be a Trader.


--- Look ---
Displays the full description of the location you are in, together with any players present.

Usage: LOOK

LOOK can be abbreviated to L.


--- Mail ---
Lists any messages you have received, for example notifications of futures contracts that have been liquidated in your absence, or mail from your cartel-mates.

Usage: MAIL


--- Marry ---
Formally marries you to another player.

Usage: MARRY playername

Parameters: 'playername' is the name of the player you want to marry.Restrictions: You and your intended must be in the registry office on Earth.

Cost: 1 slithy tove.


--- Mood ---
Allows you to set a short description that will be displayed to other players when you enter or leave a room, or when they see you in the room.

Usage: MOOD text

Parameters: 'text' is a word or phrase describing what you want other players to see.Example: if you type 'mood With a happy grin' players will see 'With a happy grin Newbod has entered the room'.

Restrictions: Limit of 95 characters. Moods are wiped when the game is reset.

MOOD on its own reminds you what your current mood is; CLEAR MOOD removes your mood.


--- Move ---
Moves a Blish city to another star system in the cartel.

Usage: MOVE cityname TO systemname

Parameters: 'cityname' is the name of the city you want to move'Systemname' is the destination star system.Example: move nutbush city to limits

Restrictions: Plutocrats only. The destination star system must be in your cartel.


--- Movement commands ---
There are twelve different movement commands - the eight points of the compass, abbreviated to their initial letters:

N

NEESESSWWNWYou can also move:

UP

DOWNINOUTWhich can be abbreivated to U, D and O (IN cannot be shortened).

Restrictions: you will only move if there is an exit that way; otherwise you will either bang your head on the wall, or perhaps something more sinister may happen...


--- Offer ---
Offers a hauling job to a Commander or Captain, with the goods coming from the exchange of the planet you are on.

Usage: OFFER playername JOB commodity planetname

Parameters: 'playername' is the recipient of the job'commodity' is the goods to be shifted'planetname' is the destination planetRestrictions: you must be on one of your own planets. You cannot offer jobs if you are still a member of the Sol cartel. The recipient must not already have a pending job offer.


--- Open link ---
Opens up a closed system so players can jump to it again.

Usage: OPEN LINK

Restrictions: You must be the owner of the system. The command must be used when you are in space.


--- Open range ---
Moves your ship away from your opponent during a fight, allowing you to use missiles.

Usage: OPEN RANGE

Restrictions: You must be in close or intermediate range.


--- Output ---
Displays the factories on your planet and tells you where the output is directed.

Usage: OUTPUT

Restrictions: you must be a planet-owner, and you must be somewhere on your planet.


--- Pardon ---
Allows a player exiled from a star system to return.

Usage: PARDON playername

Parameters: 'playername' is the name of the player you want to allow back.Restrictions: Planet-owners only. You must be somewhere in your star system.


--- Pickup ---
Collects an akatari package.

Usage: PICKUP

You must be in the location which is the collection point for the package.


--- Pocket ---
Puts away an object you are carrying .

Usage: POCKET objectname

Parameters: 'objectname' is the name of the object you want to put away.See also CARRY, WEAR and DOFF, CLIP and UNCLIP.


--- Post ---
Posts a message on the electronic notice board which can be read by other players around the Galaxy.

Usage: POST message

Parameters: 'message' is the message you want to leave on the board.Example: post Can anyone give me some work?

To read the messages on the board use the READ command. To remove the latest message you have posted, use UNPOST.

POs can also post jobs onto the workboard - see POST JOB.


--- Post job ---
Allows POs to post a job to the cartel's workboard.

Usage: POST JOB commodity planetname

Parameters: 'commodity' is the trading commodity you want delivered.'planetname' is the name of the destination planet.Example: post job droids rigel 4

Restrictions: you must be on one of your own planets. You cannot post jobs if you are still a member of the Sol cartel. You can't post if the workboard already has 40 jobs on it.


--- Promote ---
Allows a planet-owner to promote to the next level at the following reset.

Usage: PROMOTE

Restrictions: Planet-owners only. You must have done the necessary infrastucture builds for the level to which you wish to promote.


--- Quickwho ---
Gives an abbreviated listing of players in the game, just showing their names.

Usage: QUICKWHO

QUICKWHO can be abbreviated to QW.

For a full listing, use WHO.


--- Quit ---
Finishes your game session.

Usage: QUIT


--- Ranks ---
Lists the game ranks, and tells you what is required for your next promotion.

Usage: RANKS

You can also find out the promotion requirements for any other rank.

Usage: RANKS rankname

Parameters: 'rankname' is the rank you want to know the requirements for.Example: ranks captain

This will tell you what your promotion requirements would be if you were a Captain.


--- Read ---
Reads the messages on the electronic notice board.

Usage: READ

This displays the last ten messages on the board.READ #

This displays a specified number of messages. For example, READ 20 will show you the last 20 messages.READ 0

This displays all the messages on the board.Use the POST command to leave a message on the board.


--- Register business ---
Registers a private business and promotes you to Industrialist.

Usage: REGISTER BUSINESS shareprice businessname

Parameters: 'shareprice' is the initial price per share'businessname' is what you want to call the businessExample: register business 8000 Newbod Enterprises

Restrictions: you must be a Trader with the required number of trader credits. You must be in the broker's on Earth.


--- Reject ---
For Commanders and Captains, rejects a job offered to them by a PO.

Usage: REJECT JOB

To accept the job, use ACCEPT.

For Industrialists, rejects a bid from a Financier to buy shares in your business.

Usage: REJECT BID bid#

Parameters: 'bid#' is the number of the bid.Example: reject bid 2

Restrictions: Industrialists only.

To approve a bid, use APPROVE.

For Plutocrats, rejects a membership bid to join your cartel.

Usage: REJECT systemname

Parameters: 'systemname' is the system you want to refuse entry into your cartel.Example: reject rigel

Restrictions: Plutocrats only. The system must be in the pending queue for your cartel. You must be in the hub system for the cartel.

To accept a bid, use ACCEPT.


--- Relay ---
Broadcasts everything that happens to you, so it appears on another player's screen.

Usage: RELAY playername|off

Parameters: 'playername' is the name of the player you want to relay to. RELAY OFF turns the relay off again.Usage: RELAY

This reminds you who you are relaying to.Usage: RELAY CHANNEL

This relays your output to the channel you are tuned to.


--- Remove sensors/jammers ---
Removes sensors from your ship.

Usage: REMOVE sensors|jammers

This removes all the sensors or jammers.'sensors|jammers' is where you specify which of the two things you want to removeUsage: REMOVE number sensors|jammers

Parameters: 'number' is the number of sensors or jammers you want to remove.'sensors|jammers' is where you specify which of the two things you want to buyExample: remove 2 jammers


--- Rent teleporter ---
Rents a teleporter for 31 days.

Usage: RENT TELEPORTER

Cost: 1 slithy tove

Restrictions: You must be a Merchant or above. You must be in Emily's Emporium of Merchanical Delights & Electronic Wizardry on The Lattice.


--- Repair ---
Repairs damage to your ship.

Usage: REPAIR SHIP

You can get an estimate of the cost of the repair.

Usage: REPAIR SHIP ESTIMATE


--- Repay ---
Repay some or all of your outstanding ship loan.

Usage: REPAY groats

Parameters: 'groats' is the amount you want to repay.


--- Repair depot ---
Repairs 5% of the decay to the specified depot.

Usage: REPAIR DEPOT planetname

Example: repair depot marsCost: 200,000 ig.

Restrictions: Manufacturers only.


--- Repair factory ---
Repairs 5% of the decay to the specified factory.

Usage: REPAIR FACTORY factory#

Parameters: 'factory#' is the number of the factory you want to repair.Cost: 500,000 ig.

Restrictions: Manufacturers only.


--- Repair ship ---
Gets an estimate for the cost to repair a damaged ship, and carries out the repairs.

Usage: REPAIR SHIP ESTIMATE

Usage: REPAIR SHIP


--- Report events ---
Switches on the notification of things which happen in the Solar System affecting exchange prices.

Usage: REPORT EVENTS

The notifications are switched off with CANCEL EVENTS.


--- Retrieve ---
Gets an object out of your ship storage locker or your display cabinet

Restrictions: to remove locker objects, you must be in your ship. For cabinets, you must be the PO of the star system you are in. You must be able to carry the object.

Use STASH to put objects in the locker or cabinet, and DISPLAY LOCKER or EXAMINE CABINET to see what is in it.


--- Save map ---
Saves any changes you have made to a planet map so they last over the reset.

Usage: SAVE MAP

Restrictions: You must be the owner of the system.


--- Say ---
Sends a message to everyone in the same location as you.

Usage: SAY message

Parameters: 'message' is what you want to say.Example: say Hello everyone

Players see: Newbod says, "Hello everyone"An alternate of this command replaces the word SAY with a single or a double quote:

Usage: 'message or 'message

Example: 'hello everyone

Example: "hello everyoneNote: no closing quote is necessary.


--- Score ---
Displays your character's details, including bank balance, loan and stats.

Usage: SCORE

SCORE can be abbreviated to SC.


--- Search ---
Searches the location for anything hidden.

Usage: SEARCH

Restrictions: A search uses up 10 stamina on the ground, and 10 fuel in space.


--- Sell bay ---
Sells goods directly from your depot to the exchange.

Usage: SELL BAY bay#

Parameters: 'bay#' is the number of the bay which contains the goods you want to sell.Example: sell bay 9

Restrictions: Industrialists and Manufacturers only. You must be in the exchange.


--- Sell commodity ---
Sells goods carried in your ship's cargo hold to a trading exchange.

Usage: SELL commodity

Parameters: 'commodity' is the item you want to sell.Example: sell alloys

Restrictions: You must be a in trading exchange. You cannot sell goods on the same planet they were bought from.


--- Set customs ---
Sets the customs rate levied against goods imported into your cartel.

Usage: SET CUSTOMS percent

Parameters: 'percent' is the percentage you want to levy, between 0 and 100.Example: set customs 20

Restrictions: Plutocrats only. You must be somewhere in your system.


--- Sell factory ---
Sells the specified factory.

Usage: SELL FACTORY factory#

Parameters: 'factory#' is the number of the factory that you want to sell.Example: sell factory 3

Restrictions: Industrialists and Manufacturers only.


--- Sell shares ---
Decreases your personal shareholding in your company.

Usage: SELL amount SHARES

Parameters: 'amount' is the number of shares you want to sell.Example: sell 10 shares

Restrictions: Manufacturers only. You can only sell 100 shares at a time, and you cannot reduce your shareholding to less than 500.

Financiers can sell shares in other companies.

Usage: SELL amount SHARES name

Parameters: 'name' is the name of the CEO or the name of the companyExample: sell 100 shares Newbod Industries

Restrictions: You can only sell 100 shares at a time.


--- Sell treasury ---
Decreases your company's treasury stock.

Usage: SELL amount TREASURY

Parameters: 'amount' is the number of shares you want the company to sell.Example: sell 10 TREASURY

Restrictions: Manufacturers only. You can only sell 100 shares at a time.


--- Sell warehouse ---
Sells the warehouse on the planet you are on.

Usage: SELL WAREHOUSE

You will receive 250,000 IG for the sale.

WAREHOUSE can be abbreviated to WARE.


--- Send mail ---
Sends a message to one or all of your fellow cartel-members.

Usage: SEND MAIL playername message

Parameters: 'playername' is the name of one of your cartel-mates, or the word 'all'.'message' is the text to send.Example: send mail pugwash I see you've had yet another riot. Sort yourself out or leave my cartel!

send mail all Cartel party next Saturday on Rigel 4 - be there or be a cube.Restrictions: You must be on one of your planets. Cartel mail is not available in the Sol cartel.

To read your mail, use MAIL.


--- Set cartel fee|bonus ---
Sets the joining fee or signing up bonus for POs that join a cartel.

Usage: SET CARTEL fee|bonus megagroats

Parameters: 'fee|bonus' lets you specify whether you are charging a fee, or paying a bonus.'megagroats' is the amount, in megs, for the fee or bonus.Example: set cartel fee 10

set cartel bonus 20Restrictions: There is a limit of 100 meg on a fee or bonus.


--- Set factory output ---
Directs the output of the factory to either the depot or the exchange.

Usage: SET FACTORY factory# OUTPUT exchange|depot

Parameters: 'factory#' is the number of the factory you want to alter'exchange' directs the output to the exchange and 'depot' stores it in the depot.Example: set factory 4 output exchange

Restrictions: Industrialists and Manufacturers only.


--- Set factory status ---
Mothballs the specified factory so it no longer runs, or starts it up again.

Usage: SET FACTORY factory# STATUS stop|run

Parameters: 'factory#' is the number of the factory you want to stop or start'stop' stops the factory and 'run' starts it again.Example: set factory 4 status stop

Restrictions: Industrialists and Manufacturers only.


--- Set factory wages ---
Sets the level of wages you will pay for your factory workthings.

Usage: SET FACTORY factory# WAGES amount

Parameters: 'factory#' is the number of the factory you are setting the wages for'amount' is the groats you are willing to pay the workthings.Example: set factory 3 wages 40

Restrictions: Industrialists and Manufacturers only.


--- Set production ---
Tools up a Blish city to produce specified commodities, using the first free production slot.

Usage: SET PRODUCTION cityname TO commodityname

Parameters: 'cityname' is the name of the city.'Commodityname' is the name of the commodity you want to produce.Example: set production nutbush city to furs

Restrictions: Plutocrats only. The commodity must match the city's economic level.

To stop the production, use STOP PRODUCTION.


--- Set spread ---
Sets the spread between buying and selling prices in your planet's exchange.

Usage: SET SPREAD amount

Parameters: 'amount' is the gap between the buying and selling prices that you want to set.Example: set spread 25

You can also set the spread for individual commodities:

Usage: SET SPREAD amount commodity

Restrictions: The spread must be between 6 and 40. You must be somewhere on your planet.

The command can also be used remotely:

Usage: SET SPREAD amount planetname

SET SPREAD amount commodity planetnameParameters: 'planetname' is the name of your planet.


--- Set stockpile ---
Sets the minimum and maximum stock levels you want your exchange to have, either for the exchange as a whole or for individual commodities.

Usage: SET STOCKPILE max|min amount

SET STOCKPILE max|min amount commodityParameters: 'max' will set the highest amount the stockpile should go, and 'min' the lowest, 'commodity' is the name of the commodity (leave it off and the command applies to the whole exchange), and 'amount' is maximum stock you want.Example: set stockpile max 5000

Example: set stockpile min 200 livestockThe command can also be used remotely:

Usage: SET STOCKPILE max|min amount planetname

SET STOCKPILE max|min amount commodity planetnameExample: set stockpile max 5000 rigel 4

Example: set stockpile min 200 livestock rigel 4Restrictions: The max level must be between 20,000 and 200. Min must be between 100 and 2,000.


--- Set yard ---
Sets the markup for ships sold on your planet.

Usage: SET YARD amount

Parameters: 'amount' is the markup on the standard ship price, between -10 and 10. A negative number will lower the price to purchasers; a positive number will make ships more expensive.Example: set yard -5

Restrictions: You must be somewhere on your planet.


--- Shuffle ---
Rearranges the goods in your warehouse or depot to move everything down to the lowest numbered bays.

Usage: SHUFFLE

Restrictions: Merchants, Industrialists and Manufacturers only. Operates on the warehouse or depot on the planet you are on.


--- Smile ---
Smiles at everyone in the room, or at another player specifically.

Usage: SMILE

Usage: SMILE playername

Parameters: 'playername' is the name of the person you want to smile at.Note: the game adds a random qualifier.

You can smile at people who are not in the same room as you.

See also CUDDLE, GROPE, HUG, KISS, SMILE, SNOG, and TICKLE.


--- Snog ---
Snogs another player.

Usage: SNOG playername

Parameters: 'playername' is the name of the person you want to snog.Note: the game adds a random qualifier.

See also CUDDLE, GROPE, HUG, KISS, SMILE, and TICKLE.


--- Split stock ---
Doubles the number of shares in a company, with each share being half the old value.

Usage: SPLIT STOCK

Cost: 5,000ig.

Restrictions: You can only split the stock four times.


--- Sponsor fed ---
Donates some slithy toves, allowing you to directly support the running of the game.

Usage: SPONSOR FED amount

Parameters: 'amount' is the number of slithies you want to donateExample: sponsor fed 10


--- Spynet financial ---
Gives a financial report for the current game session, including company dividends that have been paid out.

Usage: SPYNET FINANCIAL


--- Spynet notice ---
Toggles on and off the notification of players entering and leaving the game.

Usage: SPYNET NOTICE

If you turn SpyNet Notice on, the notifications will last for the rest of your game session.


--- Spynet report ---
Gives you information about a player, including her gender, race, rank, ship, bank balance and whereabouts.

Usage: SPYNET REPORT playername

Parameters: 'playername' is the name of the player you want information on.


--- Spynet review ---
Lists notable events in the current game session, such as births, deaths and promotions.

Usage: SPYNET REVIEW


--- Staff ---
Displays a list of all staff members who are currently logged on.

Usage: STAFF


--- Start louie ---
Sets up a new game of Lucky Louie.

Usage: START LOUIE amount

Parameters: 'amount' is the number of groats you want to set the stake at, between 1 and 10.Example: start louie 5

Restrictions: Lucky Louie can only be played in a bar.


--- Stash ---
Puts an object into your ship storage locker or display cabinet.

Usage: STASH objectname

Parameters: 'objectname' is an object in your inventory.Restrictions: for the locker, you must be in your ship. For cabinets, you must be the PO of the star system you are in.

Use RETRIEVE to get objects back out and DISPLAY LOCKER or EXAMINE CABINET to see what is in the locker or cabinet.


--- Status ---
Displays your ship's status, including available cargo space and fuel level. If you have a job, it will remind you of the details.

Usage: STATUS

STATUS can be abbreviated to ST.


--- Stop production ---
Stops the production in a Blish city.

Usage: STOP PRODUCTION cityname slotnumber

Parameters: 'cityname' is the name of the city.'Slotnumber' is the slot you want to stop.Example: stop production nutbush 3

Restrictions: Plutocrats only.

To set up the production, use SET PRODUCTION.


--- Store ---
Moves a container of goods from your ship's cargo hold to the warehouse on the planet you are on.

Usage: STORE cargoname

Parameters: 'cargoname' is the name of the cargo you want to store.


--- Suicide ---
Use this command to kill yourself. If you are insured, this will move you to a hospital. If you are not insured, it will wipe out your Fed character completely.

Usage: SUICIDE


--- Target ---
Targets a player, in order to fire a weapon at their ship.

Usage: TARGET playername

Parameters: 'playername' is the name of the player you want to target.Example: target newbod

Remove the target with CLEAR TARGET.


--- Teleport ---
Moves you directly to another location, or another planet, provided you have a teleporter. The basic command moves you to the landing pad of the planet you are on:

Usage: TELEPORT

You can move to any location on the planet:

Usage: TELEPORT address

Parameters: 'address' is the numerical address of the location you want to move to.Example: teleport 325

You can move to the LP of another planet in the same system:

Usage: TELEPORT planetname

Parameters: 'planetname' is the planet you want to go to.Example: teleport mars

Or to a planet in another system:

Usage: TELEPORT systemname.planetname

Parameters: 'systemname' is the star system and 'planetname' is the planet you want to go to.Example: teleport rigel.rigel 4

Restrictions: You must be in possession of a teleporter, which is only available to Merchants and above.

You cannot teleport under any of these circumstances:TELEPORT can be abbreviated to TP.

To find out a teleport address, use ADDRESS.


--- Tell (TB) ---
Sends a private message to a named player, or allows you to talk to a mobile.

Usage: TELL playername message

Parameters: 'playername' is the name of the player you want to talk to; 'message' is what you want to say.Example: tell newbod Hello, are you a girl or a boy?

The recipient sees: Your comm unit signals a tight beam message from Dork, "Hello, are you a girl or a boy?"Usage: TELL mobilename message

Parameters: 'mobilename' is the name of the mobile you want to talk to; 'message' is what you want to say.Example: tell priest hello

TELL can be abbreviated to TB.


--- Termwidth ---
Formats the output text to the specified terminal width, wrapping the lines.

Usage: TERMWIDTH ##

Parameters: '##' is the width you want to set.You cannot set a termwidth of less than 40. The setting lasts until the end of your game session. To turn off the termwidth, use TERMWIDTH 0.


--- Tickle ---
Tickles another player.

Usage: TICKLE playername

Parameters: 'playername' is the name of the person you want to tickle.Note: the game adds a random qualifier.

See also CUDDLE, GROPE, HUG, KISS, SMILE, and SNOG.


--- Time ---
Displays the time (local to where the servers are, ie eastern time), the stardate, and how long you have been in the game.

Usage: TIME


--- Transfer (Xfer) ---
Moves money from your personal bank balance into your planet's treasury, or between the treasuries of any two of your planets. Plutocrats can also move money from your personal bank balance into the cartel treasury.

Usage: TRANSFER megagroats

Parameters: 'megagroats' is the number of meg you wish to transfer.Example: transfer 10

Cost: The transfer is taxed at a rate of one third.

Restrictions: You must be somewhere on your planet. You cannot transfer more than 100 meg.

Usage: TRANSFER megagroats planetname

Parameters: 'megagroats' is the number of meg you wish to transfer.'planetname' is the planet where you want the groats to move to.Example: transfer 10 bodopolis

There is no tax on this kind of transfer.

Restrictions: You must own both the planet you are standing on (which is where the groats come from) and the destination planet. You cannot transfer more than 100 meg.

Usage: TRANSFER megagroats CARTEL

Parameters: 'megagroats' is the number of meg you wish to transfer.Example: transfer 10 cartel

There is no tax on this kind of transfer.

Restrictions: Plutocrats only. You cannot transfer more than 100 meg.

TRANSFER can be abbreviated to XFER.


--- Transform slithies ---
A way for planet-owners to finance builds: it converts 4 slithies toves to 10 meg which is placed in the planet's treasury.

Usage: TRANSFORM SLITHIES

Restrictions: You must be somewhere on your planet. You can only use this facility once every 2 weeks per planet.


--- Transmit (XT) ---
Sends a message to the communications channel you are tuned to.

Usage: TRANSMIT message

Parameters: 'message' is what you want to say.TRANSMIT can be abbreviated to XMIT or XT.


--- Unblock ---
Takes the communication block off a player.

Usage: UNBLOCK playername

Parameters: 'playername' is the no-longer annoying player you want to receive messages from.Example: unblock dork.


--- Unclip ---
Removes an object from your keyring.

Usage: UNCLIP

See also CLIP, WEAR and DOFF, CARRY and POCKET.


--- Undivert ---
Removes the diversion on commodities, so instead of being diverted to the graving dock warehouse, they are put into the exchange stocks as normal.

Usage: UNDIVERT

Restrictions: Plutocrats only. You must have a graving dock.


--- Unpost ---
Removes your latest message from electronic notice board. Keep using it to remove older ones.

Usage: UNPOST


--- Update email ---
Changes the registered email address on your account.

Usage: UPDATE EMAIL new_email

Parameters: 'new_email' is what you want the email address to change to.


--- Update password ---
Changes the password for your account.

Usage: UPDATE PASSWORD new_password

Parameters: 'new_password' is what you want the password to change to.Restrictions: the password must be between 8 and 15 characters. Letters and numbers only.


--- Upgrade airport ---
Upgrades airports on a leisure planet so they can move workthings between planets in the star system.

Usage: UPGRADE AIRPORT

Cost - 5 slithy toves.

Restrictions: you must be a magnate, and you must have built ten airports.

Once the airports are upgraded, use the ASSIGN command to move the workthings.


--- Upgrade depot ---
Increases the number of bays in the depot on the planet you are on.

Usage: UPGRADE DEPOT

Cost: 500,000 ig to add one more floor.

Restrictions: Industrialists and Manufacturers only. You need a permit to upgrade the depot more than once. You must be in an exchange.


--- Upgrade factory ---
Increases the efficiency of the specified factory.

Usage: UPGRADE FACTORY factory#

Parameters: 'factory#' is the number of the factory you want to upgrade.Cost: 1,000,000 ig for a 5% increase.

Restrictions: Manufacturers only. You need a permit to increase the efficiency more than once. Efficiency can be increased to 150%.


--- Upgrade storage ---
Increases the storage capacity of the specified factory.

Usage: UPGRADE STORAGE factory#

Parameters: 'factory#' is the number of the factory for which you want to upgrade the storage.Cost: 250,000 ig for a 75 ton increase.

Restrictions: Manufacturers only. You need a permit to increase the storage more than once. Storage can only be increased to 450 tons.


--- Version ---
Displays the file version number of the planet map or space map.

Usage: VERSION

Restrictions: you must be in your star system.


--- Void ---
Cancels a job you have accepted to haul cargo, or an akaturi job.

Usage: VOID

Restrictions: you must have an outstanding job.

You will be fined for wasting Armstrong Cuthbert's time.


--- Wear ---
Displays an object in your inventory so that other players see it when they look at you.

Usage: WEAR objectname

Parameters: 'objectname' is the name of the object you want to display when other players examine you.Take it off again with DOFF. See also CARRY and POCKET, CLIP and UNCLIP.


--- Whereis ---
Tells you which system a planet is in.

Usage: WHEREIS planetname

Parameters: 'planetname' is the name of the planet you want to FIND.Example: whereis planet cabbage


--- Who ---
Lists all the players currently in the game, or those on a specific planet.

Usage: WHO

A shorter version can be obtained with QUICKWHO.

Usage: WHO planetname

Parameters: 'planetname' is the name of the planet you are interested in.Usage: WHO rank

Parameters: 'rank' is the name of the rank you want the display to be limited to.


--- Work ---
Displays the workboard from which you can accept jobs.

Usage: WORK

============================================================
CHAPTER: PLANET SCRIPTING REFERENCES
============================================================

--- Overview ---
The following are scripting commands Planet Owners can use when creating planets. See the ##LINK|150.10|Planetary Construction## section for an overview of this process.


--- ANNOUNCE ---
Sends a text message which will be broadcast in a specified location.Parameters:Location - The location number in which the message should be broadcastLow Message - The first paragraph number from the message file you want to send. Leave blank if you want to specify the text in the scriptHigh Message - The last paragraph number you want to send. Leave this blank if you only want to send one paragraph, or if you are specifying the text in the scriptMessage Text - The text to send. Leave blank if you are sending paragraphs from the message fileExample:announce type single: location 778: low port.announce.1


--- CALL ---
Calls another event.Parameters:Event to Call - The number of the event you want to call.Example:call script: event objects.jukebox.2To use with random events, replace the event number with the random call: random[a-b] where "a" is the lowest number in the range and "b" the highest number.Example:call script: event objects.jukebox.random[2-5]


--- CHANGELINK ---
Changes a movement link on the map.Parameters:Location # - The location the changed link refers toExit direction - The direction of the link you want to change: north, north east, etcAction - Whether the script should add or remove a link. It defaults to "add"New Location - Where the new movement leads to, if you are adding a locationExamples:changelink script:  location 345:  exit north:  action add:  to location 346changelink script:  location 345:  exit north:  action remove


--- CHANGEMONEY ---
Changes the player's bank balance by a specified amount, either positive or negative.Parameters:Amount - The number of groats you want to add or subtractExample:changemoney script: amount -92Restriction:You cannot add or subtract more than 1,000 groats. If adding, the gift is subject to the 1,000 per day limit for the player.


--- CHANGEPLAYER ---
Changes one or more of the player's four stats.Parameters:Stamina - The amount to change the player's staminaStrength - The amount to change the player's strengthDexterity - The amount to change the player's dexterityIntelligence - The amount to change the player's intelligenceIf you do not want an event to be called for one of the possibilities, leave the parameter blank.Examples:changeplayer script: stamina 5changeplayer script: stamina -150changeplayer script: dexterity -5: intelligence -5


--- CHANGESIZE ---
Changes the size of an object by either adding or subtracting from it, or setting it to a specific size.Parameters:ID or Name - The object whose size you want to changeChange by  - The value you want to change the size by, or to, either positive or negativeHow to change - How the change should be applied: "Add to size" (the default) or "Set to size"Examples:changesize script:  id-name milk: amount -1: change using addchangesize script:  id-name holo-card: amount 3: change using set


--- CHECKFOROWNER ---
Checks if the player is the owner of the planet and calls a different event depending on the outcome of the check.Parameters:Owner -The event to call if the player is the owner.Visitor - The event to call if the player is not the owner.Example:checkforowner script: visitor event moves.keepout.2


--- CHECKGENDER ---
Checks the gender of the player and calls a different event depending on the outcome of the check.Parameters:Male - The event number to call if the player is maleFemale - The event number to call if the player is femaleNeuter - The event number to call if the player is neuterIf you do not want an event to be called for one of the possibilities, leave the parameter blank.Example:checkgender script: male event extras.bar.2: female event extras.bar.3: neuter event extras.bar.4


--- CHECKINSURANCE ---
Checks whether a player is insured and calls a different event depending on the outcome of the check.Parameters:Pass - The event to call if the player is insuredFail - The event to call if the player is not insuredIf you do not want an event to be called for one of the possibilities, leave the parameter blank.Example:checkinsurance script: fail check.insure.2


--- CHECKINVENTORY ---
Checks the player's inventory to see if the specified object is in it, and calls a different event depending on the outcome of the check.Parameters:Map Name - the map name of the object you want to check for. Defaults to "home", otherwise you will need to use the full pathway ie newstar/bodville.ID/Name - the ID or the name of the object.Position (optional) - where the player should be holding the object. Valid options include “stored” (anywhere), “worn”, “clipped’, “held”.  If not provided, defaults to stored (anywhere).Found - the event to call if the object is present.Not Found - the event to call if the object is not present.If you do not want an event to be called for one of the possibilities, leave the parameter blank.Example:checkinventory script: map home: id-name bassoon: found objects.bassoon.2: not-found objects.basoon.3310.120 CHECKLASTLOCChecks to see whether the previous location the player was in matches that specified.Parameters:LastLocation - The location number you want to check forPass - The event to call if the player did come from that locationFail - The event to call if the player did not come from that locationIf you do not want an event to be called for one of the possibilities, leave the parameter blank.Example:checklastloc script: location 346: pass extras.bar.2


--- CHECKLOCFLAG ---
Checks the type of location the player is in, and calls a different event depending on the outcome of the check.Parameters:Flag Name - the flag you want to check for (space, line, exchange, shipyard, repair, hospital, peace, bar and custom)Flag Set Event - the event number to call if the player is in the specified type of locationFlag Not Set Event - the event to call if the player is not in the specified type of locationIf you do not want an event to be called for one of the possible outcomes, leave the parameter blank.Example:checklocflag script:  flag bar:  set objects.candle.2:  unset objects.candle.3


--- CHECKMAP ---
Checks whether the player is in a specific location, or anywhere on the specified map, and calls a different event depending on the outcome of the check.Parameters:Map Name - the name of the map - defaults to "home", otherwise you will need to use the full pathway ie newstar/bodville.Location Number - the location number; if you do not want to check for a specific location, just that the player is somewhere on the map, leave this parameter blank.Pass - the event number to call if the player is on the map or in the location.Fail - the event number to call if the player is not on the map or in the location.If you do not want an event to be called for one of the possible outcomes, leave the parameter blank.Examples:checkmap script: map newstar/bodville: pass objects.keycard.7: fail objects.keycard.6checkmap script: map home: location 851: pass objects.sargeur.8: fail objects.sargeur.6


--- CHECKMONEY ---
Checks whether a player's bank balance has a certain value and calls a different event depending on the outcome of the check.Parameters:Value to test - The number of groats you want to check forHigher - The event to call if the player's bank balance is higher than the valueEquals - The event to call if the player's bank balance is equal to the valueLower - The event to call if the player's bank balance is lower than the valueIf you do not want an event to be called for one of the possibilities, leave the parameter blank.Example:checkmoney script: amount 92: higher moves.cab.3: equals moves.cab.3: lower moves.cab.2


--- CHECKPLAYER ---
Checks the value of one or more of the player's four stats and calls a different event depending on the outcome of the check.Parameters:Stamina - The value the player's stamina needs to be to pass the checkStrength - The value the player's strength needs to be to pass the checkDexterity - The value the player's dexterity needs to be to pass the checkIntelligence - The value the player's intelligence needs to be to pass the checkPass - The event to call if the player's stats are higher or equal to all of the specified valuesFail - The event to call if one or more of the player's stats are lower than the specified valuesIf you do not want an event to be called for one of the possibilities, leave the parameter blank.Examples:checkplayer script: intelligence 35: pass gadget.use.2: fail gadget.use.3checkplayer script: stamina 30: strength 35: pass cliff.climb.2: fail cliff.climb.3


--- CHECKRANK ---
Checks the player's rank and calls a different event depending on the outcome of the check.Parameters:Rank to test - The rank you want to check forHigher - The event to call if the player is at a higher rankEquals - The event to call if the player is the same rankLower - The event to call if the player is at a lower rankIf you do not want an event to be called for one of the possibilities, leave the parameter blank.Examples:checkrank script: level merchant: lower moves.trader.2checkrank script: level founder: lower po.check.3: equals po.check.4: higher po.check.5For the level, type in the name of the rank in full, ie commander, captain etc.


--- CHECKSIZE ---
Checks an object's size to see if it is higher, lower or equal to a specified value, and calls a different event depending on the outcome of the check.Parameters:ID or Name - The object whose size is being checkedValue to Check - the object size that you want to check againstHigher - the event to call if the size is greater than the value specifiedEquals - the event to call if it's the sameLower - the event to call if it's smallerExample:checksize script: id-name holo-card: value 1: higher objects.holocard.5: equals objects.holocard.5: less object.holocard.6


--- CHECKVARIABLE ---
Example:

checkvariable script: name marsruins: key map: value iridium: equals objects.map.12


--- CLEARVARIABLE ---
Deletes the contents of a variable.Parameters:Name - The name of the variable you want to clear.Example:clearvariable script:  name marstemple


--- CREATEOBJECT ---
Creates an object or mobile from an abstract object . Objects can be created in a room or in the player's inventory.Parameters:Where - "inventory" means the object will be placed in the player's inventory (the default); "room" that it will be placed in the room the player is in.Home Map - The name of the map the abstract template is in. Defaults to "home", otherwise you will need to use the full pathway ie newstar/bodville.ID - the ID of the abstract object to be used as a template.If the object is to appear in the room then these parameters are also needed:Dest Map - the map where the object is to be placed. Defaults to "current". If you change this to anything else you will need the full pathname.Dest Location # - the location number where the object is to be placed.Examples:createobject script: where inventory: home-map home: id flower_abcreateobject script: where inventory: home-map newstar/bodville: id sausage_abcreateobject script: where room: home-map home: id flower_ab: dest-map current: dest-loc 567createobject script: where inventory: home-map home: id statue_ab: dest-map newstar/bodville: dest-loc 543


--- DELAYEVENT ---
Calls an event to be run after a specified number of seconds.Parameters:Delay - The number of seconds the delay should lastEvent - The event which should run after the delay has elapsedLog Off - The event which should run if the player is no longer in the gameExamples:delayevent script: delay 4:  event moves.cab.2delayevent script: delay 4:  event moves.cab.2  log off delay.test.3


--- DESTROYOBJECT ---
Destroys an object which has previously been created from an abstract template.Parameters:Where - "inventory", "room" or "both".Map Name - the map to which the object belongs. Defaults to "home", which means the map the events belong to.ID/Name - the name of the object to be destroyed.Example:destroyobject script: where inventory: map home: id-name sausage


--- DISPLAYSIZE ---
Sends a message which contains the size of an object.Parameters:ID or name - The object whose size you want to displayMessage text - The text to send to the player, which gives the size of the object. It should include the value %d which the game will replace with the actual sizeExample:displaysize script:  id-name milk: text 'The carton contains %d drinks of fermented llama milk, the favorite beverage on Brass.'310.240 DROPMoves an object from the ground into the player's inventory.Parameters:ID or Name - The ID or name of the object/mobileSilent? - you can suppress the message telling players they have dropped the object by specifying a silent move. This defaults to "No". If you want the move to be silent, change it to "Yes".Examples:drop script:  id-name pencildrop script:  id-name bottle:  silent yes


--- FREEZE ---
Disables a player's movement commands. To be used during a sequence of delayevents. Must be reversed with the release script.No parameters.


--- GET ---
Moves an object from the ground into the player's inventory.Parameters:ID or Name - The ID or name of the object/mobileSilent? - you can suppress the message telling players they have picked up the object by specifying a silent move. This defaults to "No". If you want the move to be silent, change it to "Yes".Examples:get script:  id-name pencilget script:  id-name bottle:  silent yes


--- MATCH ---
Checks the text a player types in when talking to a mobile; if any part of her text matches the word or phrase specified, sends one or more paragraphs from the message file, or calls an event.Parameters:ID/Name - the ID or name of the mobile.Phrase - the word or phrase to search for.Low - The first paragraph number from the message file you want to send.High - The last paragraph number you want to send.Event - the number of the event to call if the phrase does appear in the player's text.Examples:match script: id/name diesel_st: phrase hello: low objects.diesel.1match script: id/name diesel_st: phrase meaning of life: event objects.diesel.1Notes:If you just want to call an event, leave the low and high message parameters blank; if you just want to send text from the message file, leave the event parameter blank.This script is one of the few that will stop an event dead in its tracks. Usually all scripts in an event are executed, one after another; however, when the game finds a match it will stop and not check any more of the scripts in the event.


--- MESSAGE ---
Sends a message to the player. The message can be text specified in the script, or it can be one or more paragraphs from the message file.Parameters:Low - The first paragraph number from the message file you want to send. Leave blank if you want to specify the text in the scriptHigh - The last paragraph number you want to send. Leave this blank if you only want to send one paragraph, or if you are specifying the text in the scriptMessage Text - The text to send. Leave blank if you are sending paragraphs from the message fileTo whom - Which player(s) the message should go to. Defaults to "individual", ie the player that triggered the event. Can be changed to "room" or "room_ex"Examples:message script: type text: to whom individual: text 'With a buzz of static, the light goes out and the room is plunged into darkness.'message script: type text: to whom individual: text 'There is a large hole in the floor.'message script: type single: to whom individual' low extras.public.2message script: type multi: to whom individual' low extras.public.3: high extras.public.6message script: type text: to whom room: text 'With a buzz of static, the light goes out and the room is plunged into darkness. 'message script: type text: to whom room_ex: text 'Somebody has just let off a stink bomb... '


--- MOVE ---
Moves the player, or an object/mobile, to another location on the same map.Parameters:What to move - "player" or "object"Location - the location number you want the player, object or mobile to end up inFor objects and mobiles only:ID or name - The ID or name of the object/mobile, if that's what is being movedSilent (y/n) - if you are moving an object or mobile you can suppress the message telling players it has appeared or left by specifying a silent move. This defaults to "N". If you want the move to be silent, change it to "Y". For objects you would normally set it to "Y"Examples:move script: what player: to whom individual: location 31move script:  what object:  id/name policed box:  to location 1041move script:  what object:  silent yes:  id/name olice box:  to location 1041


--- NOMATCH ---
Sends one or more paragraphs from the message file or calls an event if, during a mobile conversation, the player types something that is not recognized.Parameters:ID/ Name - the ID or name of the mobile.Low - The first paragraph number from the message file you want to send.High - The last paragraph number you want to send.Event - the event to call if the player's input does not match any of the words or phrases specified.Examples:nomatch script id/name assistant_st: low keyring.assistant.4nomatch script id/name assistant_st: event keyring.assistant.9Notes:The nomatch script must come after all the match scripts in the event, because it will bring the process to a halt - the game won't search any further down the list.If you just want to call an event, leave the low and high message parameters blank; if you just want to send text from the message file, leave the event parameter blank.


--- PERCENT ---
Allows you to assign a percentage chance to something happening. The game generates a random number between 1 and 100 and checks it against your percentage, and then calls one of three different events depending on the outcome.Parameters:Value to test - The percentage you want to check againstHigher - The event to call if the random number is higher than your percentageEqual - The event to call if the random number is exactly equal to your percentageLower - The event to call if the random number is lower than your percentageExample:percent script: value 10: higher random.percent.2: equals random.percent.2: lower random.percent.3If you do not want an event to be called for any of the possible outcomes, leave the parameter blank.


--- RELEASE ---
Re-enables a player’s movement commands which have been disabled with the freeze script.No parameters.


--- SETVARIABLE ---
Sets a variable on a player, which can then be checked.Parameters:Name - The variable nameKey - The variable keyValue - The value you want to setType of event - Whether the event is temporary or permanent (defaults to temporary)Example:setvariable script:  name marsruins:  key map:  value iridium:  temporary true
